                    entry 799 create
                        action accept
                        description "0x8863/PPPoE Discovery/PADR/Others"
                        match frame-type ethernet_II
                            etype 0x8863
                        exit
                    exit
                    entry 833 create
                        action accept
                        description "0x8864/PPPoE Session/Broadcast"
                        match frame-type ethernet_II
                            dst-mac ff:ff:ff:ff:ff:ff ff:ff:ff:ff:ff:ff
                            etype 0x8864
                        exit
                    exit
                    entry 866 create
                        action accept
                        description "0x8864/PPPoE Session/Multicast"
                        match frame-type ethernet_II
                            dst-mac 01:00:5e:00:00:00 ff:ff:ff:80:00:00
                            etype 0x8864
                        exit
                    exit
                    entry 899 create
                        action accept
                        description "0x8864/PPPoE Session/Others"
                        match frame-type ethernet_II
                            etype 0x8864
                        exit
                    exit
                    entry 933 create
                        action accept
                        description "Others/Others/Broadcast"
                        match frame-type ethernet_II
                            dst-mac ff:ff:ff:ff:ff:ff ff:ff:ff:ff:ff:ff
                        exit
                    exit
                    entry 966 create
                        action accept
                        description "Others/Others/Multicast"
                        match frame-type ethernet_II

                        exit
                    exit
                    entry 999 create
                        action accept
                        description "Others/Others/Others"
                        match frame-type ethernet_II
                        exit
                    exit
                    no shutdown
                exit
            exit
        exit
    exit

#--------------------------------------------------
echo "CPM Filter Router and Svc-id Match Configuration"
#--------------------------------------------------
    system
        security
            cpm-filter
                ip-filter
                    no shutdown
                    entry 600
                        match protocol tcp
                            router Base
                        exit
                    exit
                    entry 601
                        match protocol tcp
                            router Base
                        exit
                    exit
                    entry 608
                        match protocol tcp
                            router Base
                        exit
                    exit
                    entry 609
                        match protocol tcp
                            router Base
                        exit
                    exit
                    entry 1000
                        match protocol udp
                            router Base
                        exit
                    exit
                exit
                mac-filter
                    no shutdown
                exit
            exit
        exit
    exit
#--------------------------------------------------
echo "Router (Service Side) Configuration"
#--------------------------------------------------
    router Base
#--------------------------------------------------
echo "OSPFv2 Configuration"
#--------------------------------------------------
        ospf 0
            no shutdown
        exit
#--------------------------------------------------
echo "OSPFv3 Configuration"
#--------------------------------------------------
        ospf3 0
            no shutdown
        exit
#--------------------------------------------------
echo "ISIS Configuration"
#--------------------------------------------------
        isis 0
            no shutdown
        exit
#--------------------------------------------------
echo "PIM Configuration"
#--------------------------------------------------
        pim
            no shutdown
        exit
#--------------------------------------------------
echo "Policy Configuration"
#--------------------------------------------------
        policy-options
            begin
            prefix-list "rfc1918"
                prefix 10.0.0.0/8 longer
                prefix 172.16.0.0/12 longer
                prefix 192.168.0.0/16 longer
            exit
            prefix-list "plDefaultRoute"
                prefix 0.0.0.0/0 exact
            exit
            prefix-list "plPrivateRoute "
                prefix 10.0.0.0/8 longer
